 shanivaar or ravivaar ko is dauraan wadala stesan se mumbai chhatrapati shivaji terminus ke bich local sevaayen puri tarah se thap raheen, ummid he ki hafte ke pehle kaarobaari din main musafiron ko kisi musiibat kaa saamana nahin karnaa padegaa
 There was no entry at Mumbai Chhatrapati Shivaji Terminus for trains on the Harbor Line on saturday-sunday
 104 sevaayen radd huin, trainen panwel se wadala tak hi chalin
 Taxis cut silver among the crowd, but the passengers remained upset
 is root se safar karne vaale devraj ne kaha, 'megablock kii vajah se mujhe bahut pareshaani hui
 
 
 i also work on Sundays, but the cancellation of the train made it very difficult
 ' altaaf kaa kahana tha, 'taxi vaale jane se manaa kar rahe hai, jo ja rahe hai wo meter se adhik paisa maang rahe hai
 Comments megablock ke pehle charan main siasti stesan par plateform kii lambaai lagbhag 65 meter tak badhaai gai, signlon ko bhi sthanantarit kiya gaya
 In the second phase, both the up and down routes between Wadala to CST were completely closed
 is bare main madhya rail ke mukhya jansampark adhikari narendra patil ne kaha, 'kuch signlon ko hataaya gaya he, plateform kii lambaai bhi badhaai gai, musafiron ke liye hamane vaikalpik intazaam bhi kiye
 ' siasti-wadala root par 2009 ke baad duusari baar trainen puri tarah rukii hai, us vakt 48 ghante ke liye masjid road overbrij ko giraane ke liye is root ko band kiya gaya tha
 Mumbai's Western and Central lines run 15 and 12 coaches locally, but the Harbor Line, which carries a million passengers, used to run only 9 coaches, expected to be on this route in 2-3 months after the pain of megablock
 Local coaches of 12 coaches will run and according to the promise, the quality of services will increase by 33 percent
 shanivaar-ravivaar ko horbar line kii trainon ke liye mumbai chhatrapati shivaji terminus main no entry rahi
 104 services were canceled, trains ran from Panvel to Wadala
 bheedbhad ke bich taxi waalon ne chaandi kaati, lekin musafir pareshaan rahe
 Devraj, who traveled by this route, said, 'I had a lot of trouble due to the Megablock
 
 
 main ravivaar ko bhi kaam karata hum, lekin train radd hone se bahut mushkil hui
 'altaf said,' Taxiers are refusing to go, those who are going are asking for more money than meters
 'tippaniyan In the first phase of the Megablock, the length of the platform at the CST station was increased to about 65 meters, the signals were also moved
 duusare charan main wadala se siasti ke bich ap down donon rooton ko puri tarah band rakhaa gaya
 In this regard, Central Public Relations Officer Narendra Patil said, "some of the signals have been removed, the length of the platform has also been increased, we have also made alternative arrangements for the passengers
 ' For the second time since 2009, trains on the cst-wadala route have come to a complete standstill, at that time the route was closed to demolish the Masjid Road overbridge for 48 hours
 mumbai kii western or central line par 15 or 12 dibbon kii local daudti he, lekin das lakh musafiron ko dhone vaali horbar line main sirf 9 dibbon kii local chalati thi, ummid he megablock ke dard ke baad 2-3 maheenon main is root par bhi 12 dibbon kii local daudegi or vaayade ke mutabik sevaaon kii gunvattta main 33 fisadi ijapha hoga

 wo itane bekhauf the ki police kii maujuudagi main kathith aropiyon kii pitayee karte rahe, lekin sipaahi kuch na kar sake

 thane main bhi hangamabhagava brigade kii gundgardee ke aage police itani bebas thi ki jab vah ladki or ladakon ko thane laai to vahaan bhi hindu yuva vahini ke sadasyon ne jamkar hangaamaa kiya
 Even threatened the policemen
 hindu yuva vahini kaa aarope he ki ye jabaran dharm parivartan kaa maamla he, jiske taar kashmir se jude ho sakate hai
 However, the police have taken the accused boys and girl in their custody
 punjab police ko suchit kar diya gaya he
 The echoes of the jewel scandal of Gautam Buddha Nagar are heard all over the country
 is bich peedit mahilaon ke saath gangrape hone kii baat ko siemo ne report ke aadhaar par galat bataaya tha

 ve is sambandh main magistrate ke samaksh bayaan bhi dengi

 haalanki mahilaon ke kapade FSL jaanch ke liye bhej die gaye hai
 According to the CMO, after the FSL report is received in three weeks, it will be possible to know whether the women were gangraped or not
 is khulaase ke chalate gangrape kii baat abhi tak saaf nahin he

 unhone bataaya ki unke saath badmaashon ne balaatkaar kiya tha
 She will give a statement in this regard before the Magistrate under Section 164
 mahilaon ke mutabik rape kaa virodh karne par hi badmaashon ne shakeel ko goli maari thi
 Now they need justice
 shanivaar ko magistrate ke samaksh peedit mahilaon ke bayaan darj kiye jaaenge
 Let me tell you that the UP Police is still searching for the accused in the case of jewelry
 upi police kii madad ke liye estf kii ek team ko bhi lagaaya gaya he
 Let us tell you that on Wednesday night, near the village of Sabouta in Jewar police station area of greater Noida, half a dozen armed miscreants had robbed a family in a car
 virodh karne par badmaashon ne parivaar ke mukhiya kii goli markar uski hatya kar di thi

 duniyabar main hone vaale sabhi beauty pagents main ek vijeta ke achche luks hi nahin balki uski samaj or nechar ko bhi dekha jaataa he

 are classic examples of this

 unamem sirf bade logon ke liye hi dayaa nahin thi balki unke liye bhi thi, jiske paas kuch nahin he

 hamen unase bhi badhkar dekhne kii jarurat he tabhi ek asli miss world ubharegi

 gauratlab he ki quick charge takanee snapadragon ke adar hi hogi, isliye aap jaahir he ise alag se kharid nahin sakate hai
